A BILL 
To provide an earned path to citizenship, to address the 
root causes of migration and responsibly manage the 
southern border, and to reform the immigrant visa sys-
tem, and for other purposes. 
Be it enacted by the Senate and House of Representa-
1
tives of the United States of America in Congress assembled, 
2

SEC. 2001. DEFINITIONS. 
6
In this title: 
7
(1) BEST
INTEREST
DETERMINATION.—The 
8
term ‘‘best interest determination’’ means a formal 
9
process with procedural safeguards designed to give 
10
primary consideration to the child’s best interests in 
11
decision making. 
12
(2) INTERNALLY
DISPLACED
PERSONS.—The 
13
term ‘‘internally displaced persons’’ means persons 
14
or groups of persons who— 
15
(A) have been forced to leave their homes 
16
or places of habitual residence because of armed 
17
conflict, generalized violence, violations of 
18
human rights, or natural or human-made disas-
19
ters; and 
20
(B) have not crossed an internationally 
21
recognized border of a nation state. 
22
(3) INTERNATIONAL
PROTECTION.—The term 
23
‘‘international protection’’ means— 
24
(A) asylum status; 
25
23:39 Mar 30, 2021
H1177
101 
•HR 1177 IH
(B) refugee status; 
1
(C) 
protection 
under 
the 
Convention 
2
Against Torture and Other Cruel, Inhuman or 
3
Degrading Treatment or Punishment, done at 
4
New York December 10, 1984; and 
5
(D) any other regional protection status 
6
available in the Western Hemisphere. 
7
(4) LARGE-SCALE, NONINTRUSIVE INSPECTION 
8
SYSTEM.—The term ‘‘large-scale, nonintrusive in-
9
spection system’’ means a technology, including x- 
10
ray, gamma-ray, and passive imaging systems, capa-
11
ble of producing an image of the contents of a com-
12
mercial or passenger vehicle or freight rail car in 1 
13
pass of such vehicle or car. 
14
(5) PRE-PRIMARY.—The term ‘‘pre-primary’’ 
15
means deploying scanning technology before primary 
16
inspection booths at land border ports of entry in 
17
order to provide images of commercial or passenger 
18
vehicles or freight rail cars before they are presented 
19
for inspection. 
20
(6) SCANNING.—The term ‘‘scanning’’ means 
21
utilizing nonintrusive imaging equipment, radiation 
22
detection equipment, or both, to capture data, in-
23
cluding images of a commercial or passenger vehicle 
24
or freight rail car.

SEC. 2101. UNITED STATES STRATEGY FOR ENGAGEMENT 
5
IN CENTRAL AMERICA. 
6
(a) IN GENERAL.—The Secretary of State shall im-
7
plement a 4-year strategy, to be known as the ‘‘United 
8
States Strategy for Engagement in Central America’’ (re-
9
ferred to in this subtitle as the ‘‘Strategy’’)— 
10
(1) to advance reforms in Central America; and 
11
(2) to address the key factors contributing to 
12
the flight of families, unaccompanied noncitizen chil-
13
dren, and other individuals from Central America to 
14
the United States. 
15
(b) ELEMENTS.—The Strategy shall include efforts— 
16
(1) to strengthen democratic governance, ac-
17
countability, transparency, and the rule of law; 
18
(2) to combat corruption and impunity; 
19
(3) to improve access to justice; 
20
(4) to bolster the effectiveness and independ-
21
ence of judicial systems and public prosecutors’ of-
22
fices; 
23
(5) to improve the effectiveness of civilian police 
24
forces; 
25

4
such organizations; 
5
(7) to disrupt money laundering and other illicit 
6
financial operations of criminal networks, armed 
7
gangs, illicit trafficking organizations, and human 
8
smuggling networks; 
9
(8) to promote greater respect for internation-
10
ally recognized human rights, labor rights, funda-
11
mental freedoms, and the media;

(9) to protect the human rights of environ-

(10) to enhance accountability for government

(11) to enhance the capability of governments
